#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	vec4 _BaseMap_ST;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD5;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
float u_xlat12;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat12 = max(u_xlat12, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat12 = inversesqrt(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x + (-u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat0.yzzx * u_xlat0.xyzz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(unity_SHBr, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.y = dot(unity_SHBg, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(unity_SHBb, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = unity_SHC.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(unity_SHAr, u_xlat0);
    u_xlat16_2.y = dot(unity_SHAg, u_xlat0);
    u_xlat16_2.z = dot(unity_SHAb, u_xlat0);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = (-_Smoothness) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7.x = (-u_xlat16_0.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_14 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_14);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_14) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_14 = dot((-u_xlat8.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_14 + u_xlat16_14;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_14)) + (-u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat16_14 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat16_14 = clamp(u_xlat16_14, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_14 = (-u_xlat16_14) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_14 * u_xlat16_14;
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_14 * u_xlat16_14;
    u_xlat10_1 = textureCube(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat10_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_0.y = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_7.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = max(u_xlat16_0.xy, vec2(6.10351563e-05, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_7.x = log2(u_xlat16_0.y);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_7.x = exp2(u_xlat16_7.x);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xxx;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xxx;
    u_xlat16_7.x = (-_Metallic) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_21 = (-u_xlat16_7.x) + _Smoothness;
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_21 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_21 = clamp(u_xlat16_21, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_4 = texture2D(_BaseMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * _BaseColor.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Metallic, _Metallic, _Metallic)) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_21) + (-u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_14) * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * _BaseColor.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_4.w * _BaseColor.w + _DrawObjectPassData.w;
    SV_Target0.w = clamp(SV_Target0.w, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xxx * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = max(u_xlat22, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat22 = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = clamp(u_xlat22, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);

    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;

    u_xlat22 = max(u_xlat16_24, 0.100000001);
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x + -1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat9 + 1.00001001;

    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x;

    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat22 + -6.10351563e-05;

    u_xlat16_0.x = min(u_xlat16_0.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
float u_xlat12;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat12 = max(u_xlat12, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat12 = inversesqrt(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x + (-u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat0.yzzx * u_xlat0.xyzz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(unity_SHBr, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.y = dot(unity_SHBg, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(unity_SHBb, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = unity_SHC.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(unity_SHAr, u_xlat0);
    u_xlat16_2.y = dot(unity_SHAg, u_xlat0);
    u_xlat16_2.z = dot(unity_SHAb, u_xlat0);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
float u_xlat4;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x + (-u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat0.yzzx * u_xlat0.xyzz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(unity_SHBr, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.y = dot(unity_SHBg, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(unity_SHBb, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = unity_SHC.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(unity_SHAr, u_xlat0);
    u_xlat16_2.y = dot(unity_SHAg, u_xlat0);
    u_xlat16_2.z = dot(unity_SHAb, u_xlat0);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat4 = u_xlat0.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat4 = min(max(u_xlat4, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat4 = clamp(u_xlat4, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    gl_Position = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.x = u_xlat4;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.yzw = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;

varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD5;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    gl_Position = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.x = u_xlat1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.yzw = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

#define SV_Target0 gl_FragData[0]
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;

float u_xlat11;
mediump float u_xlat16_12;
mediump float u_xlat16_18;
mediump float u_xlat16_27;

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = (-_Smoothness) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_9.x = (-u_xlat16_0.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_9.x = u_xlat16_9.x * u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat16_9.x = u_xlat16_9.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_18 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_18);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_18) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_18 = dot((-u_xlat10.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_18 = u_xlat16_18 + u_xlat16_18;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_18)) + (-u_xlat10.xyz);
    u_xlat16_18 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat10.xyz);
    u_xlat16_18 = clamp(u_xlat16_18, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_18 = (-u_xlat16_18) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_18 = u_xlat16_18 * u_xlat16_18;
    u_xlat16_18 = u_xlat16_18 * u_xlat16_18;
    u_xlat10_1 = textureCube(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_9.x);
    u_xlat16_9.x = u_xlat10_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_0.y = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_9.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = max(u_xlat16_0.xy, vec2(6.10351563e-05, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_9.x = log2(u_xlat16_0.y);
    u_xlat16_9.x = u_xlat16_9.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_9.x = exp2(u_xlat16_9.x);
    u_xlat16_9.x = u_xlat16_9.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xxx;
    u_xlat16_9.x = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_9.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_9.x;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xxx;
    u_xlat16_9.x = (-_Metallic) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_27 = (-u_xlat16_9.x) + _Smoothness;
    u_xlat16_27 = u_xlat16_27 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_27 = clamp(u_xlat16_27, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_4 = texture2D(_BaseMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * _BaseColor.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Metallic, _Metallic, _Metallic)) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_27) + (-u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_18) * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat10_7.xyz = texture2D(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat10_7.xyz + u_xlat10_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * _BaseColor.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_4.w * _BaseColor.w + _DrawObjectPassData.w;
    SV_Target0.w = clamp(SV_Target0.w, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat28 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat28 = max(u_xlat28, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat28 = inversesqrt(u_xlat28);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat28) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat28 = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat28 = clamp(u_xlat28, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat16_12 = u_xlat28 * u_xlat28;
    u_xlat28 = max(u_xlat16_12, 0.100000001);
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x + -1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat11 + 1.00001001;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat28 = u_xlat28 * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_0.x * 4.0 + 2.0;
    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat28 = u_xlat28 * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat28 = u_xlat16_0.x / u_xlat28;
    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat28 + -6.10351563e-05;
    u_xlat16_0.x = max(u_xlat16_0.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_0.x = min(u_xlat16_0.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat28 = unity_LightData.z * unity_ProbesOcclusion.x;
    u_xlat16_27 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat28;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_27) * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + (-unity_FogColor.xyz);
    SV_Target0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD6.xxx * u_xlat16_0.xyz + unity_FogColor.xyz;
    return;

{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    gl_Position = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.x = u_xlat1.x;

    return;

vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

#ifdef FRAGMENT

#ifdef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
    precision highp float;
#else
    precision mediump float;

precision highp int;
uniform 	vec4 _MainLightPosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainLightColor;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _DrawObjectPassData;

uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainLightShadowOffset3;

uniform lowp sampler2D _BaseMap;
uniform lowp sampler2D unity_Lightmap;
uniform highp sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
uniform lowp samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;

varying highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD5;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
#define SV_Target0 gl_FragData[0]
vec4 u_xlat0;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
bool u_xlatb1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
lowp vec3 u_xlat10_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
bool u_xlatb9;
float u_xlat10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_13;
float u_xlat27;
mediump float u_xlat16_30;
mediump float u_xlat16_31;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat0.xy).x;
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat0.x<u_xlat0.z;
    u_xlat0.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat1.xy).x;
    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat1.x<u_xlat1.z;
    u_xlat0.y = (u_xlatb1) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat1.xy).x;
    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat1.x<u_xlat1.z;
    u_xlat0.z = (u_xlatb1) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat1.xy).x;
    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat1.x<u_xlat1.z;
    u_xlat0.w = (u_xlatb1) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_11.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_11.x;
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
    u_xlatb9 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb9 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat0.x = unity_LightData.z * unity_ProbesOcclusion.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat16_11.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_11.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_11.x);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat16_11.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot((-u_xlat9.xyz), u_xlat16_11.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x + u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * (-u_xlat16_2.xxx) + (-u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat16_11.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.x = clamp(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_2.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_30 = (-_Smoothness) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_31 = (-u_xlat16_30) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat16_30;
    u_xlat16_30 = max(u_xlat16_30, 6.10351563e-05);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 * 6.0;
    u_xlat10_0 = textureCube(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat10_0.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_4.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = exp2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat16_30 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_31 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-_Metallic) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_13.x = (-u_xlat16_4.x) + _Smoothness;
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_13.x = clamp(u_xlat16_13.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_5 = texture2D(_BaseMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat10_5.xyz * _BaseColor.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Metallic, _Metallic, _Metallic)) * u_xlat16_6.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xxx + (-u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat16_13.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_13.xyz;
    u_xlat10_7.xyz = texture2D(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat10_7.xyz + u_xlat10_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat10_5.xyz * _BaseColor.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_5.w * _BaseColor.w + _DrawObjectPassData.w;
    SV_Target0.w = clamp(SV_Target0.w, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat16_11.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = clamp(u_xlat27, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.100000001);
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat16_30 + -1.0;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat10 + 1.00001001;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat27;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_30 * 4.0 + 2.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat16_30;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat27 * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat16_2.x / u_xlat27;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat27 + -6.10351563e-05;
    u_xlat16_2.x = max(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = min(u_xlat16_2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    return;
}

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_25);
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-_Metallic) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_11.x = (-u_xlat16_4.x) + _Smoothness;
    u_xlat16_11.x = u_xlat16_11.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_11.x = clamp(u_xlat16_11.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_5 = texture2D(_BaseMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat10_5.xyz * _BaseColor.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(vec3(_Metallic, _Metallic, _Metallic)) * u_xlat16_6.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);

    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat16_11.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat10_5.xyz * _BaseColor.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_5.w * _BaseColor.w + _DrawObjectPassData.w;
    SV_Target0.w = clamp(SV_Target0.w, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = clamp(u_xlat21, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.100000001);

    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat21;

    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_24 * u_xlat16_24;
